is one of the most played board games in the world, play with your friends, try to defeat your opponents with strategy, reasoning and a little bit of luck.\r\nGeneral rules of dominoes:\r\n- Blocking game\r\nThe most basic dominos variant is for two players and requires a double six set. The 28 domino tiles are shuffled face down and form the stock or boneyard. Each player draws seven tiles; the remainder are not used. Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board Game.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9MTCC9265B2B","TileLayout":"Poster","Title":"Candy Fever : Fun Puzzle Match 3 Game","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.23428.13810706148961729.1a5a49ea-20dc-464a-b513-4959262c7770.f364c527-60cc-4cb6-8f6a-ecd9154a4470","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.1744.13810706148961729.dc42c7f9-7bf5-4b2a-b6fc-86237e031c7a.5bf4c2ae-2ec2-4329-b358-555f9bf854dc","Height":300,"Width":620,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Bezplatné","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":4.0,"RatingsCount":"3","PackageFamilyNames":["46728SweetCandyKingdom.CandyFeverFunPuzzleMatch3Ga_ncv0abr25ncwe"],"ContentIds":["3189d4d4-97c3-5cec-085c-2d120f2d47cd","935ecffb-3130-6f36-418e-2137a1d196f2"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"SWAP, CRUSH and MATCH 3 or more same magic candies to master the fun of casual match-3 game. V júni 1968 vydanie Scientific American, Martin Gardner opísal vo svojej \"Matematické Games\" stĺpec hru Cl Bakera, ktorý je podobný FreeCell, okrem toho, že karty na tablo sú postavené farby skôr než alternatívnymi farbami. Gardner napísal: \"Hra bola učil Baker jeho otec, ktorý na oplátku ju naučil od Angličana v roku 1920.\" Tento variant sa teraz nazýva Baker je hra. Freecell pôvody môžu sa datujú ešte do roku 1945, a škandinávsky hra s názvom Napoleon v St. Helena (nie hra Napoleon pri St. Helena, tiež známy ako štyridsať lúpežníkov).\r\n\r\nPaul Alfille zmenil Bakerov hru tým, že karty stavať podľa alternatívnych farbách, tak vytvárať FreeCell. On realizovala prvú počítačovú verziu tom v TUTOR programovacieho jazyka pre PLATO vzdelávacieho počítačového systému v roku 1978. Alfille bol schopný ľahko zobraziť rozpoznateľné grafické obrázky hracie karty na displeji 512 * 512 monochromatické na PLATO systémoch.\r\n\r\nTento originálny FreeCell prostredie povolená hry s 4C10 stĺpy a 1C10 buniek okrem štandardného 8 * 4 hru. Pre každý variant, program uložený zoradených zoznam hráčov, s najdlhšou víťazné pruhmi. Tam bol tiež turnaj systém, ktorý dovolil ľuďom súťažiť vyhrať ťažké ručne vybral ponuky. Pavel Alfille opisuje túto skorú FreeCell prostredia podrobnejšie v rozhovore z roku 2000.\r\n\r\n\r\nRiešiteľ zložitosť\r\nFreeCell Hra má konštantný počet kariet. To znamená, že v konštantnom čase, človek alebo počítačový mohli vymenovať všetkých možných ťahov z danej konfigurácii začiatku a objavte víťaznú sadu pohybov, alebo za predpokladu, že hru nie je možné riešiť, je jeho nedostatok. Ak chcete vykonať zaujímavou zložitosť analýzu je potrebné postaviť všeobecný verziu hry FreeCell so 4 * n kariet. Táto zovšeobecnená verzia hry je NP-úplný; to je nepravdepodobné, že by akýkoľvek algoritmus efektívnejšie než hľadanie brute-force existuje, ktoré môžete nájsť riešenie pre svojvoľné všeobecných konfigurácie FreeCell.\r\n\r\nExistujú 52! (Tj, 52 faktoriál), alebo približne 8 * 1067, odlišné zaoberá. Avšak, niektoré hry sú v podstate zhodné s ostatnými, pretože obleky priradené ku kartám sú svojvoľné alebo stĺpce môžu byť zamenené.
